  DATASET
  {
    { 1100285500;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11072003;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               TEMPDimValueChains@1100285501 : TEMPORARY Record 11128020;
                               First@1100285500 : Boolean;
                             BEGIN
                               GLSetup.GET;
                               FilterCostCenter := '';
                               IF DimensionCode = GLSetup."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code" THEN BEGIN

                                 FilterCostCenter := DimensionValueCode;

                               END ELSE BEGIN

                                 IF DimensionValueCode <> '' THEN
                                   TEMPDimValueChains.getSourceDimensions(DimensionCode, DimensionValueCode, GLSetup."Shortcut Dimension 1 Code", TEMPDimValueChains);

                                 First := TRUE;
                                 IF TEMPDimValueChains.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN REPEAT

                                   IF First THEN BEGIN
                                     FilterCostCenter := TEMPDimValueChains."Start Dimension Value Code";
                                     First := FALSE
                                   END ELSE
                                     FilterCostCenter += '|' + TEMPDimValueChains."Start Dimension Value Code";
                                 UNTIL TEMPDimValueChains.NEXT = 0;

                                END;
                               SETFILTER(Job."Global Dimension 1 Code",FilterCostCenter);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  DummyRec@1100285500 : Record 11072021;
                                BEGIN
                                  //Rensa fÑlt
                                  CLEAR(Year);
                                  CLEAR(Month);
                                  CLEAR(Datetxt);
                                  CLEAR(ProjectPreclosureResult);
                                  CLEAR(TotRevProg);
                                  CLEAR(TotCostProg);
                                  CLEAR(Job2);
                                  CLEAR(Ofak);
                                  CLEAR(CLE);
                                  CLEAR(JLE);
                                  CLEAR(RemAmount);
                                  CLEAR(TotRevProgNew);
                                  CLEAR(TotCostProgNew);
                                  CLEAR(Dim1txt);
                                  CLEAR(PTDesc);
                                  CLEAR(GLEntry);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedNewCost);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedOldCost);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedNewRev);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedOldRev);
                                  CLEAR(RemAmountNew);
                                  CLEAR(Omvrld);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedOldCostFil);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedOldCostTim);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedNewCostFil);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedNewCostTim);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedPreRes2013);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedPreRes2014);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedPreRes2013Old);
                                  CLEAR(ClosedPreRes2014Old);
                                  CLEAR(ProjectPreclosureResultClosed);
                                  CLEAR(CalcTurnover);
                                  CLEAR(CalcTurnoverNew);
                                  CLEAR(CalcCost);
                                  CLEAR(CalcCostNew);
                                  CLEAR(OfakNew);
                                  CLEAR(DirectCost2);
                                  CLEAR(DirectCost2New);
                                  CLEAR(EBITA);
                                  CLEAR(EBITANew);
                                  //>>160211 ITERO.SB
                                  CLEAR(ActPreRes);
                                  CLEAR(CalcPreRes);
                                  //<<
                                  IF Period<> 0D THEN BEGIN
                                    Datetxt2 := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(Period,3)) + '-' + FORMAT(DATE2DMY(Period,2));
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    Period:=DMY2DATE(1,DATE2DMY(TODAY,2),DATE2DMY(TODAY,3));//TODAY;
                                    Datetxt2 := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(Period,3)) + '-' + FORMAT(DATE2DMY(Period,2));
                                  END;
                                  Job.SETFILTER("Period Filter",'..%1',Period);
                                  Job.SETFILTER("Cumulation Filter",'..%1',Period);
                                  Datetxt3 := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)) + '-' + FORMAT(DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),2));

                                  //SlutmÜnad
                                  IF Job."Ending Date"<>0D THEN BEGIN
                                    Datetxt := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(Job."Ending Date",3)) + '-' + FORMAT(DATE2DMY(Job."Ending Date",2));
                                  END;

                                  //èr
                                  DateIntY := DATE2DMY(Period,3);

                                  IF PT.GET(Job."Project Type") THEN
                                    PTDesc:=PT.Description
                                  ELSE
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  //Sista bokfîrda vÑrdering i fîregÜende mÜnad.
                                  Job2.GET(Job."No.");
                                  ProjectPreclosureResult.SETRANGE("Project No.",Job2."No.");
                                  //IF Period<> 0D THEN
                                  //  ProjectPreclosureResult.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'<%1',Period);

                                  ProjectPreclosureResult.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',CALCDATE('-1M',
                                  DMY2DATE(1,DATE2DMY(Period,2),DATE2DMY(Period,3))),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));


                                  //MESSAGE('%1',ProjectPreclosureResult.GETFILTER(ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date"));
                                    ProjectPreclosureResult.SETRANGE(Posted,TRUE);
                                  IF ProjectPreclosureResult.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                                    Job2.SETFILTER("Period Filter",'..%1',ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date");
                                    Job2.SETFILTER("Cumulation Filter",'..%1',ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date");
                                    TotRevProg:=ProjectPreclosureResult."Prognosis Total Revenues";
                                    TotCostProg:=ProjectPreclosureResult."Prognosis Total Cost";
                                    IF TotRevProg<>0 THEN
                                      EBITA:=((TotRevProg-TotCostProg)/TotRevProg)*100;
                                    CalcTurnover:=ProjectPreclosureResult."Calculated Turnover";
                                    CalcPreRes:=ProjectPreclosureResult."Calculated Preclosure Result";
                                    //ActPreRes:=ProjectPreclosureResult."Actual Preclosure Result";
                                    CalcCost:=ProjectPreclosureResult."Calculated Cost";
                                    //Datetxt3 := FORMAT(DATE2DMY(ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date",3)) + '-' + FORMAT(DATE2DMY(ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date",2));

                                    CLEAR(JLE3);
                                    JLE3.SETRANGE("Job No.",Job2."No.");
                                    JLE3.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',CALCDATE('-1M',
                                    DMY2DATE(1,DATE2DMY(Period,2),DATE2DMY(Period,3))),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                    JLE3.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                    ActPreRes:=JLE3."Actual Preclosure Result";

                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    Job2.SETFILTER("Period Filter",'..%1',CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                    Job2.SETFILTER("Cumulation Filter",'..%1',CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));

                                  END;


                                    //CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  Job2.CALCFIELDS("Project Contract Amount","Extension Contract Amount",
                                  Revenues,"Actual Costs","Closed Costs","Closed Revenues");

                                  Ofak:=(Job2."Actual Costs" + Job2."Closed Costs") - (Job2.Revenues - Job2."Closed Revenues" );

                                  //Ej betalda fakturor
                                  CLE.SETRANGE("Project No.",Job2."No.");
                                  CLE.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'..%1',CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));///ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date");
                                  CLE.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
                                  CLE.CALCSUMS("Sales (LCY)");
                                  RemAmount:=CLE."Sales (LCY)";
                                  //IF CLE.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                  //  CLE.CALCFIELDS("Sales (LCY)");
                                  //  RemAmount:=RemAmount+CLE."Sales (LCY)";
                                  //UNTIL CLE.NEXT=0;
                                  //Kostnader
                                  //Direkt kostnad
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'..%1',CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));//ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date");
                                  //JLE.SETRANGE("Job No.",Job2."No.");
                                  JLE.SETRANGE("Main Project No.",Job2."No.");
                                  //JLE.SETFILTER("No.",'%1|%2|%3|%4',PT."Closed Subcontracting Credit",PT."Closed Plant Credit",PT."Closed Material Credit",PT."Closed Labor Credit");
                                  //JLE.CALCSUMS("Total Cost (LCY)");
                                  //DirectCost2:=JLE."Total Cost (LCY)";
                                  //Tim
                                  JLE.SETRANGE("No.",PT."Closed Sundry Credit");
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1|%2|%3','9901','9902','9998');
                                  JLE.CALCSUMS("Total Cost (LCY)");
                                  Tim2:=JLE."Total Cost (LCY)";
                                  //Filial
                                  JLE.SETRANGE("No.",PT."Closed Sundry Credit");
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1|%2','9903','9999');
                                  JLE.CALCSUMS("Total Cost (LCY)");
                                  FilOmkost:=JLE."Total Cost (LCY)";
                                  IF CalcCost<>0 THEN
                                    DirectCost2:=CalcCost-(Tim2+FilOmkost);
                                  //Resultat 2013
                                  CLEAR(JLE);
                                  JLE.SETRANGE("Job No.",Job2."No.");
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',(DMY2DATE(1,1,(DATE2DMY(Period,3)-1))),(DMY2DATE(31,12,(DATE2DMY(Period,3)-1))));//ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date");
                                  JLE.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                  //MESSAGE(JLE.GETFILTERS);
                                  ResPrevY:=JLE."Actual Preclosure Result";
                                  //Simulera vÑrdering idag
                                  Ok:=FALSE;
                                  IF Job."Preclosure Result"<>Job."Preclosure Result"::No THEN BEGIN
                                    GetProject();
                                    IF Ok THEN BEGIN
                                      CalculateResult(ProjPreclResultRec, DummyRec, FALSE);
                                      //MESSAGE('Datum: %1 Upparbet: %2 OmsÑttning: %3 Kostnad: %4',ProjPreclResultRec."Posting Date",ProjPreclResultRec."Progress %",ProjPreclResultRec.Turnover,ProjPreclResultRec.Cost);

                                      TotRevProgNew:=ProjPreclResultRec."Prognosis Total Revenues";
                                      TotCostProgNew:=ProjPreclResultRec."Prognosis Total Cost";
                                      IF TotRevProgNew<>0 THEN
                                        EBITANew:=((TotRevProgNew-TotCostProgNew)/TotRevProgNew)*100;

                                      CalcTurnoverNew:=ProjPreclResultRec."Calculated Turnover";
                                      CalcPreResNew:=ProjPreclResultRec."Calculated Preclosure Result";
                                      ActPreResNew:=ProjPreclResultRec."Actual Preclosure Result";
                                      ActPreResNew2:=ActPreResNew;
                                      CalcCostNew:=ProjPreclResultRec."Calculated Cost";

                                      CLEAR(JLE3);
                                      JLE3.SETRANGE("Job No.",Job2."No.");
                                      JLE3.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,DATE2DMY(Period,2),DATE2DMY(Period,3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',Period));//ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date");
                                      JLE3.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                      //MESSAGE(JLE3.GETFILTERS);
                                      ActPreResNew:=ActPreResNew+JLE3."Actual Preclosure Result";

                                    END;

                                  END;

                                  Job.CALCFIELDS("Project Contract Amount","Extension Contract Amount",
                                  Revenues,"Actual Costs","Closed Costs","Closed Revenues");

                                  OfakNew:=(Job."Actual Costs" + Job."Closed Costs") - (Job.Revenues - Job."Closed Revenues" );

                                  CLEAR(CLE);
                                  CLEAR(JLE);
                                  //Ej betalda fakturor
                                  CLE.SETRANGE("Project No.",Job."No.");
                                  CLE.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'..%1',Period);
                                  CLE.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
                                  CLE.CALCSUMS("Sales (LCY)");
                                  RemAmountNew:=CLE."Sales (LCY)";
                                  //IF CLE.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                  //  CLE.CALCFIELDS(CLE."Sales (LCY)");
                                  //  RemAmountNew:=RemAmountNew+CLE."Sales (LCY)";
                                  //UNTIL CLE.NEXT=0;
                                  //Kostnader
                                  //Direkt kostnad
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'..%1',Period);
                                  //JLE.SETRANGE("Job No.",Job."No.");
                                  JLE.SETRANGE("Main Project No.",Job."No.");
                                  //JLE.SETFILTER("No.",'%1|%2|%3|%4',PT."Closed Subcontracting Credit",PT."Closed Plant Credit",PT."Closed Material Credit",PT."Closed Labor Credit");
                                  //JLE.CALCSUMS("Total Cost (LCY)");
                                  //DirectCost2New:=JLE."Total Cost (LCY)";

                                  JLE.SETRANGE("No.",PT."Closed Sundry Credit");
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1|%2|%3','9901','9902','9998');
                                  JLE.CALCSUMS("Total Cost (LCY)");
                                  Tim2New:=JLE."Total Cost (LCY)";

                                  JLE.SETRANGE("No.",PT."Closed Sundry Credit");
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1|%2','9903','9999');
                                  JLE.CALCSUMS("Total Cost (LCY)");
                                  FilOmkostNew:=JLE."Total Cost (LCY)";

                                  IF CalcCostNew<>0 THEN
                                    DirectCost2New:=CalcCostNew-(Tim2New+FilOmkostNew);


                                  IF "Dimension Value".GET(GLSetup."Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code") THEN
                                    Dim1txt:="Dimension Value".Name;


                                  JobTemp.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                  JobTemp.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                  IF NOT JobTemp.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    //Avslutade projekt
                                    IF PT.GET(Job."Project Type") THEN BEGIN
                                      GLEntry.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");

                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1|%2|%3|%4',PT."Closed Labor Debit",PT."Closed Material Debit",PT."Closed Subcontracting Debit",PT."Closed Plant Debit");
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedOldCost:=GLEntry.Amount;

                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1',PT."Closed Sundry Debit");
                                      //GLEntry.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1|%2','9901','9902');
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedOldCostTim:=GLEntry.Amount;

                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1',PT."Closed Sundry Debit");
                                      //GLEntry.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1','9903');
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedOldCostFil:=GLEntry.Amount;

                                      GLEntry.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 2 Code");
                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1',PT."Closed Revenue Credit");
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedOldRev:=GLEntry.Amount*-1;

                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(Period,3)),Period);
                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1|%2|%3|%4',PT."Closed Labor Debit",PT."Closed Material Debit",PT."Closed Subcontracting Debit",PT."Closed Plant Debit");
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedNewCost:=GLEntry.Amount;

                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1',PT."Closed Sundry Debit");
                                      //GLEntry.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1|%2','9901','9902');
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedNewCostTim:=GLEntry.Amount;

                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1',PT."Closed Sundry Debit");
                                      //GLEntry.SETFILTER("Global Dimension 2 Code",'%1','9903');
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedNewCostFil:=GLEntry.Amount;


                                      GLEntry.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 2 Code");
                                      GLEntry.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1',PT."Closed Revenue Credit");
                                      GLEntry.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                      ClosedNewRev:=GLEntry.Amount*-1;
                                      //MESSAGE(Job."No.");

                                      JobTemp.INIT;
                                      JobTemp."No.":=Job."No.";
                                      JobTemp.INSERT(FALSE);    //JobTemp.INSERT(TRUE);  IME428
                                      JobTemp."Global Dimension 1 Code":=Job."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                      JobTemp."Project Type":=Job."Project Type";
                                      JobTemp.MODIFY(FALSE);    //JobTemp.MODIFY(TRUE);  IME428

                                      //Aktuellt Ür
                                      //>>160211 ITERO.SB
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.CALCFIELDS("Project Status","Project Type");
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETRANGE("Project Status",ProjectPreclosureResultClosed."Project Status"::Finished);
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                      //<<
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(Period,3)),Period);
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                      ClosedPreRes2014:=ProjectPreclosureResultClosed."Actual Preclosure Result";

                                      //FîregÜende Ür
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',(DMY2DATE(1,1,(DATE2DMY(Period,3)-1))),
                                      (DMY2DATE(31,12,(DATE2DMY(Period,3)-1))));
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                      ClosedPreRes2013:=ProjectPreclosureResultClosed."Actual Preclosure Result";

                                      //Aktuellt Ür
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETRANGE("Project Status",ProjectPreclosureResultClosed."Project Status"::Finished);
                                      //>> 160211 ITERO.SB
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                      //<<
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                      ClosedPreRes2014Old:=ProjectPreclosureResultClosed."Actual Preclosure Result";

                                      //FîregÜende Ür
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',(DMY2DATE(1,1,(DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)-1))),
                                      (DMY2DATE(31,12,(DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)-1))));//ProjectPreclosureResult."Posting Date");
                                      ProjectPreclosureResultClosed.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                      ClosedPreRes2013Old:=ProjectPreclosureResultClosed."Actual Preclosure Result";

                                    END;
                                  END;
                                  //OmvÑrldsanalys
                                  IF (TotCostProg+DirectCost2New+FilOmkostNew+Tim2New)<>0 THEN
                                    Omvrld:=CalcPreResNew-(TotRevProg*(DirectCost2New+FilOmkostNew+Tim2New)/(TotCostProg+DirectCost2New+FilOmkostNew+Tim2New));


                                  //Resultat Aktuellt Ür, tom aktuell mÜnad
                                  CLEAR(JLE);
                                  JLE.SETRANGE("Job No.",Job2."No.");
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(Period,3)),Period);
                                  JLE.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                  ResActYNew:=JLE."Actual Preclosure Result"+ActPreResNew2;

                                  //Resultat Aktuellt Ür, tom fîregÜende mÜnad
                                  JLE.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                  JLE.CALCSUMS("Actual Preclosure Result");
                                  ResActYPrev:=JLE."Actual Preclosure Result";
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Project Type,Bill-to Customer No.,Contract Type,Project Status,Single/Main/Sub Project }

      { 1100285502;1;Field  ;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Dimension;
                             NOR=Dimensjon;
                             SVE=Dimension];
                  SourceExpr=DimensionCode;
                  OnLookup=VAR
                             Dimension@1100285000 : Record 348;
                           BEGIN
                             IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, Dimension) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
                               DimensionCode := Dimension.Code;
                             RequestOptionsPage.UPDATE;
                           END;
                            }

      { 1100285501;1;Field  ;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Dimension Value;
                             NOR=Dimensjonsverdi;
                             SVE=DimensionsvÑrde];
                  SourceExpr=DimensionValueCode;
                  OnLookup=VAR
                             DimensionValue@1100285000 : Record 349;
                           BEGIN
                             DimensionValue.SETRANGE("Dimension Code", DimensionCode);
                             IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, DimensionValue) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
                               DimensionValueCode := DimensionValue.Code;
                             RequestOptionsPage.UPDATE;
                           END;
                            }

    }
  }

    { 1100285507;Kontrakt      ;CaptionML=SVE=Kontrakt (EBITA %) }

    PROCEDURE GetProject@1100285500();
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(ProjPreclResultRec);
      ResultType:=ResultType::Preclosure;
      //IF Period <> 0D THEN
      PostingDate:=Period;
      //ELSE
      //  PostingDate:=TODAY;
      AddNew:=TRUE;

      IF Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD" = Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD"::No THEN
        EXIT;//CurrReport.SKIP;

      IF (Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD" = Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD"::"Preclosure Result") AND
         (ResultType = ResultType::Provision) THEN
        EXIT;//CurrReport.SKIP;

      IF (Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD" = Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD"::"Provision Loss") AND
         (ResultType = ResultType::Preclosure) THEN
        EXIT;//CurrReport.SKIP;

      ProjPreclResultRec.RESET;
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.","Line No.");
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
      LineNo := 10000;  //Select new lineno.
      IF ProjPreclResultRec.FINDLAST THEN
        LineNo := ProjPreclResultRec."Line No." + 10000;

      ProjPreclResultRec.RESET;
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.","Posting Date","Line No.");
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE("Project No.",Job."No.");
      //ProjPreclResultRec.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '>%1', PostingDate);
      //IF ProjPreclResultRec.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN   //Only when there are not entries with newer posting dates
      //  ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE("Posting Date", PostingDate);
      //  ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE(Posted, FALSE);
      //  IF ProjPreclResultRec.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN   //Only when there are no entries on posting date which are not posted
      //    ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE(Posted, TRUE);
      //    IF ProjPreclResultRec.ISEMPTY OR AddNew THEN BEGIN
            ProjPreclResultRec.RESET;

            IF ResultType = ResultType::Provision THEN
              IF ProjPreclResultRec.CheckPreclResultPresent011(FALSE) THEN
                EXIT;
                //CurrReport.SKIP;

            ProjPreclResultRec.INIT; //** Call C010248
            ProjPreclResultRec."Project No.":= Job."No.";
            ProjPreclResultRec.VALIDATE("Line No.", LineNo);
            ProjPreclResultRec."Posting Date":= PostingDate;
            ProjPreclResultRec."Result Type" := ResultType;
            ProjPreclResultRec."Prognosis Level" := Job."Prognosis Level"; //C000501

            IF ProjPreclResultRec.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
              Ok:=TRUE;

      //    END;
      //  END;
      //END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateResult@1100525001(VAR IProjPreclResultRec@1100525002 : TEMPORARY Record 11012093;IProjRecordingLine@1100525004 : Record 11072021;ICalledFromProjectRecording@1100525003 : Boolean);
    VAR
      lvDampingRatioRec@1100525001 : Record 11072019;
      lvHoldPreclRec@1100525006 : TEMPORARY Record 11012093;
      lvPrognRevenuePresent@1100525000 : Boolean;
      lvPrognRevenue@1100525007 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      WITH IProjPreclResultRec DO BEGIN
        JobSetup.GET; //Function can be called from outside
        TESTFIELD(Posted, FALSE);
        lvHoldPreclRec := IProjPreclResultRec;
        INIT; //Clear previous calculations and other progress fields
        "Result Type" := lvHoldPreclRec."Result Type";
        "Global Dimension 1 Code" := lvHoldPreclRec."Global Dimension 1 Code";

        JobRec.GET("Project No.");
        JobRec.SETFILTER("Cumulation Filter", '..%1', "Posting Date");
        JobRec.SETRANGE("Period Filter", "Posting Date");

        DetermineProgressDate.DetermineBothDates(JobRec,FALSE);
        DeterminePrognosisDate.DetermineBothDates(JobRec);

        JobRec.FillProjectFilter(ProjFilter);
        JobRec.SETFILTER("Project Filter", ProjFilter);
        JobRec.CALCFIELDS(
          "Actual Costs",
          "Project Contract Amount",
          "Extension Contract Amount",
          "Options Contract Amount");

        CLEAR(PrognosisRec);
        "Prognosis Total Cost" := 0;
        IF JobSetup."Purch. Result in Precl. Result" THEN
          "Purchase Result" := CostContMgt.PurchResultProject(JobRec, TRUE);
        "Prognosis Total Revenues" := 0;
        "Prognosis Financial Result" := 0;
        IF JobRec.GETFILTER("Prognosis Filter") <> '' THEN BEGIN
          PrognosisRec.SETRANGE("Project No.", "Project No.");
          PrognosisRec.SETFILTER("Prognosis Date", JobRec.GETFILTER("Prognosis Filter"));
          IF PrognosisRec.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            IF PrognosisRec."Prognosis Level" = PrognosisRec."Prognosis Level"::Rough THEN BEGIN
              "Prognosis Total Cost" := PrognosisRec."Rough Prognosis Total Cost";
              "Prognosis Total Revenues" := PrognosisRec."Rough Prognosis Total Revenues";
              lvPrognRevenuePresent := "Prognosis Total Revenues" <> 0;
      //>>4PS-002
            //END ELSE BEGIN
            END ELSE
              IF JobRec."Forecast Level" = JobRec."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component" THEN BEGIN
                PrognosisRec.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Total Revenue CC", "Prognosis Total Cost CC");
                "Prognosis Total Cost" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Total Cost CC";
                "Prognosis Total Revenues" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Total Revenue CC";// + PrognosisRec."Project Invoiced";
                "Purchase Result" := 0;
                //>> 140514 ITERO.SB IME-145
                PrognosisRec.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Revenue CC");
                //<<
                lvPrognRevenuePresent := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Revenue CC" <> 0;
              END ELSE
      //>>4PS-002
            BEGIN
              PrognosisRec.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Revenue", "Prognosis Total Cost");
              "Prognosis Total Cost" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Total Cost";
              "Prognosis Total Revenues" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Revenue" + PrognosisRec."Project Invoiced";
              lvPrognRevenuePresent := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Revenue" <> 0;
            END;
            "Prognosis Financial Result" := "Prognosis Total Revenues" - ("Prognosis Total Cost" + "Purchase Result") ;
          END;
        END;
        "Actual Cost" := JobRec."Actual Costs" ;
        "Contract Amount" :=
          JobRec."Project Contract Amount" +
          JobRec."Extension Contract Amount" +
          JobRec."Options Contract Amount";

        //IF lvPrognRevenuePresent THEN
          lvPrognRevenue := "Prognosis Total Revenues";
        //ELSE
        //  lvPrognRevenue := "Contract Amount";

        IF ICalledFromProjectRecording THEN
          PrognEndResVersusContractPr := IProjRecordingLine."Progn. End Res. Vs. Contract"
        ELSE BEGIN
          PrognEndResVersusContractPr := CostContMgt.PrognEndResVrsContrAmtProject(JobRec, TRUE);
        END;
        IF lvPrognRevenuePresent THEN
          PrognEndResVersusContractPr := PrognEndResVersusContractPr - "Contract Amount" + "Prognosis Total Revenues";

        CALCFIELDS("Previous Actual Precl. Result", "Prev. Actual Preclosure Rev.", "Prev. Actual Preclosure Cost");

        "Progress % Base" := 0;

        CASE JobRec."Preclosure Result" OF
          JobRec."Preclosure Result"::Allowed,
          JobRec."Preclosure Result"::"Sales Allowed":
            IF ICalledFromProjectRecording THEN
              "Progress % Base" := IProjRecordingLine.Progress
            ELSE
              "Progress % Base" := CostContMgt.AllowedPercProject(JobRec,TRUE);
          JobRec."Preclosure Result"::Invoiced: //08-07-09
            BEGIN
              JobRec.CALCFIELDS(Revenues);
      //M C-027051 so
      //        IF JobRec."Project Contract Amount" + JobRec."Extension Contract Amount" + JobRec."Options Contract Amount" <> 0 THEN
      //          "Progress % Base" :=
      //            JobRec.Revenues /
      //            (JobRec."Project Contract Amount" + JobRec."Extension Contract Amount" + JobRec."Options Contract Amount") * 100
      //M C-027051 sn
              IF lvPrognRevenue <> 0 THEN
                "Progress % Base" := (JobRec.Revenues / lvPrognRevenue) * 100;
      //M C-027051 en
            END;
          ELSE
            IF JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress" = JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress"::"Cost to Revenue" THEN BEGIN
              IF lvPrognRevenue <> 0 THEN
                "Progress % Base" :=  ("Actual Cost"/lvPrognRevenue) * 100;
            END;
            IF JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress" = JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress"::"Cost to Cost" THEN BEGIN
              IF (lvPrognRevenue - PrognEndResVersusContractPr <> 0) THEN
                "Progress % Base" := ("Actual Cost"/(lvPrognRevenue-PrognEndResVersusContractPr)) * 100;
            END;
            //C-026777.sn
            IF JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress" = JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress"::"Cost to Cost (incl. Firm Commitments)" THEN BEGIN
              IF (lvPrognRevenue - PrognEndResVersusContractPr <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                JobRec.CALCFIELDS("Received/Not Invoiced", "Open Ovh. Surch. Firm (Purch.)");  // C-026777
                FirmCommitments := JobRec."Received/Not Invoiced" + JobRec."Open Ovh. Surch. Firm (Purch.)";  // C-026777
                "Progress % Base" := (("Actual Cost" + FirmCommitments)/(lvPrognRevenue-PrognEndResVersusContractPr)) * 100;
              END;
            END;
            //C-026777.en
        END;

        IF (JobRec."Preclosure Result" = JobRec."Preclosure Result"::"Sales Progress") OR
           (JobRec."Preclosure Result" = JobRec."Preclosure Result"::"Sales Allowed") THEN BEGIN

          IF gvCountUnits THEN BEGIN
            PlotRec.RESET;
            PlotRec.SETRANGE("Project No.", JobRec."No.");
            "Units Saleable" := PlotRec.COUNT;
            PlotRec.SETFILTER("Sales Status", '%1..', PlotRec."Sales Status"::Sold);
            PlotRec.SETFILTER("Sales Status Since", '..%1', "Posting Date");
            "Units Sold" := PlotRec.COUNT;
          END;

          IF "Units Saleable" <> 0 THEN
            "Sales Progress" := ROUND(100 * "Units Sold" / "Units Saleable")
          ELSE
            "Sales Progress" := 0;
          "Progress %" := ROUND("Progress % Base" * ("Sales Progress" / 100));
        END ELSE
          "Progress %" := "Progress % Base";

      //>>4PS-002
        IF JobRec."Forecast Level" = JobRec."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component" THEN BEGIN
          "Progress % Base" := 0;
          IF "Prognosis Total Cost" <> 0 THEN
            "Progress % Base" := (JobRec."Actual Costs" / "Prognosis Total Cost" * 100);
          "Progress %" := "Progress % Base";
        END;
      //>>4PS-002

      //>> 150604 ITERO.SB IME-366 Change calculation of Progress for cost object level
        IF JobRec."Forecast Level" = JobRec."Forecast Level"::"Cost Object" THEN BEGIN
          "Progress % Base" := 0;
          IF "Prognosis Total Cost" <> 0 THEN
            "Progress % Base" := (JobRec."Actual Costs" / "Prognosis Total Cost" * 100);
          "Progress %" := "Progress % Base";
        END;
      //<<

        IF "Progress %" > 100 THEN  //M16746
          "Progress %" := 100;      //M16746

        //>> 150608 ITERO.SB IME-366 Change calculation of Progress
        IF "Progress %" < 0 THEN BEGIN
          IF ("Prognosis Total Cost" > 0) AND (JobRec."Actual Costs" < 0) THEN
            "Progress %" := 0;
        END;

        IF "Progress %" < 0 THEN BEGIN
          IF ("Prognosis Total Cost" < 0) AND (JobRec."Actual Costs" > 0) THEN
            "Progress %" := 0;
        END;
        //>>


        IF "Result Type" = "Result Type"::"Preclosure Result" THEN BEGIN
          "Expected Final Result" := "Prognosis Financial Result";
          "Corrected Final Result":= "Expected Final Result";
          "Calculated Turnover" := ROUND("Progress %" * lvPrognRevenue / 100);
          "Actual Preclosure Revenue" := "Calculated Turnover" - "Prev. Actual Preclosure Rev.";

          IF "Expected Final Result" < 0 THEN
            "Calculated Preclosure Result" := "Expected Final Result"
          ELSE BEGIN
            "Calculated Preclosure Result" := "Progress %" * "Expected Final Result" / 100 ;
            lvDampingRatioRec.SETFILTER("Until Production", '>=%1', ROUND("Progress %", 1, '>'));
            IF lvDampingRatioRec.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              "Calculated Preclosure Result" := "Progress %" * lvDampingRatioRec.Ratio * "Expected Final Result" / 100;
            END;
          END;

          "Calculated Preclosure Result" := ROUND("Calculated Preclosure Result");
          "Corrected Preclosure Result" := "Calculated Preclosure Result" ;
          "Actual Preclosure Result" := "Calculated Preclosure Result" - "Previous Actual Precl. Result";
          "Actual Preclosure Result" := ROUND("Actual Preclosure Result");

          "Calculated Cost" := ROUND("Calculated Turnover" - "Calculated Preclosure Result");
          "Corrected Preclosure Cost" := "Calculated Cost";
          "Actual Preclosure Cost" := ROUND("Corrected Preclosure Cost" - "Prev. Actual Preclosure Cost");
          "Progress % Actual" := "Progress %";  //C001798.n
        END ELSE BEGIN
          "Progress % Actual" := 0;  //C001798.n
          IF "Prognosis Financial Result" < 0 THEN
            "Calculated Provision" := "Prognosis Financial Result"
          ELSE
            "Calculated Provision" := 0;

          CALCFIELDS("Previous Actual Provision");
          "Actual Provision" := "Calculated Provision" - "Previous Actual Provision"
        END;

        "Prognosis Date" := JobRec.GETRANGEMAX("Prognosis Filter");
        "Progress Date" := JobRec.GETRANGEMAX("Progress Filter");
        "Prognosis Level" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Level";
        MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      160211 ITERO.SB IME-452 & RFC-107
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
